## synonym:backward
- reverse
- rear
- rearward
- back
- backwards

## synonym:female_person
- lady
- girl
- woman
- female

## synonym:forward
- forth
- front
- along
- onward
- ahead

## synonym:male_person
- boy
- man
- gentleman
- male
- dude
- guy

## synonym:pointing left
- pointing to the right

## synonym:pointing right
- pointing to the left

## synonym:rising left arm
- raising their left arm

## synonym:rising right arm
- raising their right arm
